[Location]: After all, in the county, if you are not traveling by car, it is recommended to live near West Street, which is convenient for taking a taxi. The hotel is at the entrance of West Street, but the balcony door of the room is relatively thick, and the outside sound cannot be heard at all when it is closed, and it is very soundproof.
*[Traffic]: There are too many people on West Street, so there will be traffic control on several roads at night. Fortunately, the hotel is at the entrance of West Street. We got off the bus and walked a few steps there. If you live in a hotel in West Street, you may have to walk more.
[Room]: The hotel is clean, and the attitude of the staff is very good. What's more considerate is that the few clothes I washed were originally placed on the stool on the balcony. When I came back at night, I found that there was an extra floor-to-ceiling hanger on the balcony, and all the clothes were hung on the hanger. The only suggestion that needs to be improved is the shower head. The shower head cannot be moved up and down.
[Food]: There are many things to eat in West Street. [Master Beer Fish] has many branches in West Street, and there is one in front of the hotel. It is delicious. Those who like to eat snail noodles strongly recommend [Aimin snail noodles] in West Street. It takes 5 minutes to walk and the door opens at 8:30 in the morning. Don't eat the noodles on the street opposite the hotel, one family tastes worse than the other, and you stepped on mine twice. I went in and asked 2 tourists who said it was delicious, so I dared to order it.
[Others]: 1. Do not buy tickets online for Eternal Love! ! ! There are a lot of scalpers at the entrance of the scenic spot, and you can cut it down to 160-180 yuan. There are enough VIP seats, so let them book area A, facing the stage, near the front! Those with children can bring swimsuits, and there are water games inside. Key point: The opening time of the scenic spot is not fixed every day, which is very tricky. We went early and waited for a long time. Based on the time of the first performance, the doors will open about 1 hour earlier.
2. Yulong River rafting tickets are hard to grab. The official account grabs the ticket and enters the payment interface. After entering the verification code, it will always display "loading". Don't worry, don't log out, and be patient. I just have no experience. I quit and re-entered but didn‚Äôt get it. In the end, I bought a scalper and added more money.
3. Shili Gallery: Although the sidecars look good in photos, they are not easy to ride, difficult to turn around, and they are not allowed on the road, they can only be driven in trails, and there are still many people riding electric vehicles.
